${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k}{-{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$ ; ${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} = {{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}{-{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}}$;${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ d} _k} _j} _l}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
symmetrizing indexes
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{-1}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{-1}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ d} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{-1}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

Ricci curvature

using ${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

using Ricci definition

${{\frac{\partial { {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _x} _x}}{\partial t}} + {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{ {{ b} _x} _z}}}{-{{ {{ b} _z} _x}}} + {{{2}} {{{ {{ {\hat{d}_t}} _x} _z}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ d} _x} _x} _z}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^y}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _y} _x} _z}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^y}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ d} _y} _x} _z}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^z}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _x} _z}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^z}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ d} _z} _x} _z}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ {{ K} _x} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}\right)}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _x} _y}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^y}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _x} _x} _z}}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _x} _z}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^z}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _x} _x} _z}}}}}} = {S}$

${{\frac{\partial { {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _y} _z}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^z}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _x} _y} _z}}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _z} _z} _z}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^z}}} \cdot {{{ {{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _x} _z} _z}}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _x} _x}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _x} _x}}}}} + {{{{ { a} _x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}} + {{{{ { d} _x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ { e} _x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}} + {{{{ {{{ d} ^x} _x} _x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _x} _x} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { Z} _x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _x} _y}}{\partial t}} + {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{{ { a} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}} + {{{{ { d} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ { e} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _x} _y} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _y} _x} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { Z} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _x} _y}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ {{{ d} ^x} _x} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}\right)}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _x} _z}}{\partial t}} + {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{{ { a} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}} + {{{{ { d} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ { e} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _x} _z} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _z} _x} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { Z} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _x} _z}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ {{{ d} ^x} _x} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}\right)}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _y} _y}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _y} _y}}}}} + {{{{ {{{ d} ^x} _y} _y}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _y} _y} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _y} _z}}{\partial t}} + {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{{ {{{ d} _y} _z} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _z} _y} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _y} _z}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ {{{ d} ^x} _y} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}\right)}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial { {{ K} _z} _z}}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{{ {{ K} _z} _z}}}}} + {{{{ {{{ d} ^x} _z} _z}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ {{{ d} _z} _z} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}} = {S}$
${{\frac{\partial \Theta}{\partial t}}{-{{{{ { Z} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}{-{{{{ { \beta} ^x}}} \cdot {{\Theta}}}} + {{{{ { d} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}{-{{{{ { e} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}} = {S}$

${{\frac{\partial { { Z} _z}}{\partial t}}{-{\left({{{{{ { Z} _z}}} \cdot {{{ { \beta} ^x}}}} + {{{{ {{ K} _z} ^x}}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}\right)}}} = {S}$

${\frac{\partial { {{ b} ^z} _y}}{\partial t}} = {S}$
${\frac{\partial { {{ b} ^z} _z}}{\partial t}} = {S}$

flux:
flux->a_l.x = -beta_u.x * a_l.x + K * alpha * f + -2. * Theta * alpha * f;
flux->a_l.y = -beta_u.y * a_l.x;
flux->a_l.z = -beta_u.z * a_l.x;
flux->dDelta_lll.xxx = -b_ll.xx + dHat_t_ll.xx + -beta_u.x * d_lll.xxx + beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.yxx + -beta_u.y * d_lll.yxx + beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.zxx + -beta_u.z * d_lll.zxx + K_ll.xx * alpha;
flux->dDelta_lll.xxy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xxx;
flux->dDelta_lll.xxz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xxx;
flux->dDelta_lll.xyy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xxy;
flux->dDelta_lll.xyz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xxy;
flux->dDelta_lll.xzz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xxz;
flux->dDelta_lll.yxx = (-b_ll.xy + -b_ll.yx + 2. * dHat_t_ll.xy + -2. * beta_u.x * d_lll.xxy + 2. * beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.yxy + -2. * beta_u.y * d_lll.yxy + 2. * beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.zxy + -2. * beta_u.z * d_lll.zxy + 2. * K_ll.xy * alpha) / 2.;
flux->dDelta_lll.yxy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xxy;
flux->dDelta_lll.yxz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xxy;
flux->dDelta_lll.yyy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xyy;
flux->dDelta_lll.yyz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xyy;
flux->dDelta_lll.yzz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xyz;
flux->dDelta_lll.zxx = (-b_ll.xz + -b_ll.zx + 2. * dHat_t_ll.xz + -2. * beta_u.x * d_lll.xxz + 2. * beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.yxz + -2. * beta_u.y * d_lll.yxz + 2. * beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.zxz + -2. * beta_u.z * d_lll.zxz + 2. * K_ll.xz * alpha) / 2.;
flux->dDelta_lll.zxy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xxz;
flux->dDelta_lll.zxz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xxz;
flux->dDelta_lll.zyy = -beta_u.y * dDelta_lll.xyz;
flux->dDelta_lll.zyz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xyz;
flux->dDelta_lll.zzz = -beta_u.z * dDelta_lll.xzz;
flux->K_ll.xx = -beta_u.x * K_ll.xx + a_l.x * alpha + d_l.x * alpha + -e_l.x * alpha + d_ull.xxx * alpha + -d_llu.xxx * alpha + -2. * Z_l.x * alpha;
flux->K_ll.xy = (a_l.y * alpha + d_l.y * alpha + -e_l.y * alpha + -d_llu.xyx * alpha + -d_llu.yxx * alpha + -2. * Z_l.y * alpha + -2. * beta_u.x * K_ll.xy + 2. * d_ull.xxy * alpha) / 2.;
flux->K_ll.xz = (a_l.z * alpha + d_l.z * alpha + -e_l.z * alpha + -d_llu.xzx * alpha + -d_llu.zxx * alpha + -2. * Z_l.z * alpha + -2. * beta_u.x * K_ll.xz + 2. * d_ull.xxz * alpha) / 2.;
flux->K_ll.yy = -beta_u.x * K_ll.yy + d_ull.xyy * alpha + -d_llu.yyx * alpha;
flux->K_ll.yz = (-d_llu.yzx * alpha + -d_llu.zyx * alpha + -2. * beta_u.x * K_ll.yz + 2. * d_ull.xyz * alpha) / 2.;
flux->K_ll.zz = -beta_u.x * K_ll.zz + d_ull.xzz * alpha + -d_llu.zzx * alpha;
flux->Theta = -Z_u.x * alpha + -beta_u.x * Theta + d_u.x * alpha + -e_u.x * alpha;
flux->Z_l.x = -Z_l.x * beta_u.x + -K_lu.xx * alpha + K * alpha + -Theta * alpha;
flux->Z_l.y = -(Z_l.y * beta_u.x + K_lu.yx * alpha);
flux->Z_l.z = -(Z_l.z * beta_u.x + K_lu.zx * alpha);
flux->beta_u.x = 0.;
flux->beta_u.y = 0.;
flux->beta_u.z = 0.;
flux->b_ul.xx = -beta_u.x * b_ul.xx + -beta_u.y * b_ul.xy + -beta_u.z * b_ul.xz + a_u.x * alpha * alpha + d_u.x * alpha * alpha + -2. * e_u.x * alpha * alpha;
flux->b_ul.xy = 0.;
flux->b_ul.xz = 0.;
flux->b_ul.yx = -beta_u.x * b_ul.yx + -beta_u.y * b_ul.yy + -beta_u.z * b_ul.yz + a_u.y * alpha * alpha + d_u.y * alpha * alpha + -2. * e_u.y * alpha * alpha;
flux->b_ul.yy = 0.;
flux->b_ul.yz = 0.;
flux->b_ul.zx = -beta_u.x * b_ul.zx + -beta_u.y * b_ul.zy + -beta_u.z * b_ul.zz + a_u.z * alpha * alpha + d_u.z * alpha * alpha + -2. * e_u.z * alpha * alpha;
flux->b_ul.zy = 0.;
flux->b_ul.zz = 0.;
